SELECT (
    SELECT SUM([t2].[c])
    FROM (
        SELECT MAX([e3].[ActualPoints]) AS [c]
        FROM [Submissions] AS [e3]
        INNER JOIN (
            SELECT [e4].*
            FROM [Problems] AS [e4]
            WHERE [e4].[IsDeleted] = 0
        ) AS [t1] ON [e3].[ProblemId] = [t1].[Id]
        WHERE (([e3].[IsDeleted] = 0) AND (([e3].[UserId] = @__userId_0) AND ([t1].[IsExtraTask] = 0))) AND ([t].[Id] = [e3].[ContestId])
        GROUP BY [e3].[ProblemId]
    ) AS [t2]
) AS [ActualPoints], (
    SELECT SUM([e5].[MaxPoints])
    FROM [Problems] AS [e5]
    WHERE (([e5].[IsDeleted] = 0) AND ([e5].[IsExtraTask] = 0)) AND ([t0].[Id] = [e5].[LessonId])
) AS [MaxPoints], [t].[Name] AS [ContestName], [t].[LessonId], [x.UserContests].[ContestId]
FROM [AspNetUsers] AS [e]
INNER JOIN [UserContests] AS [x.UserContests] ON [e].[Id] = [x.UserContests].[UserId]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [e0].*
    FROM [Contests] AS [e0]
    WHERE [e0].[IsDeleted] = 0
) AS [t] ON [x.UserContests].[ContestId] = [t].[Id]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [e1].*
    FROM [Lessons] AS [e1]
    WHERE [e1].[IsDeleted] = 0
) AS [t0] ON [t].[LessonId] = [t0].[Id]
WHERE ((([e].[IsDeleted] = 0) AND ([e].[IsDeleted] = 0)) AND ([e].[Id] = @__userId_0)) AND ((
    SELECT COUNT(*)
    FROM [Problems] AS [e2]
    WHERE ([e2].[IsDeleted] = 0) AND ([t0].[Id] = [e2].[LessonId])
) > 0)
